WebAR, on the other hand, refers to Augmented Reality experiences that are accessible through web browsers without the need for downloading dedicated apps. It allows users to access AR content directly from a web page, making AR more accessible and easier to experience without additional installations.

The contactless NFC business cards like Evrycard [3] could be a useful tool for you to streamline sharing your contact details and networking more efficiently. By simply tapping the NFC card on someone's smartphone, you can instantly transfer your information like email, phone number, social media links, and more directly to their contacts.

This eliminates the hassle of manually entering details or losing traditional paper business cards. The Evrycard website highlights how these digital cards allow you to "Share. Anything. Anywhere." and keep important connections from getting lost. [3]

To maximize the utility of this system, you could integrate it with a free Customer Relationship Management (CRM) platform like HubSpot's CRM [1]. This would allow you to centrally manage all the new contacts you collect through the NFC cards, track interactions, and nurture those relationships more effectively.

HubSpot's CRM offers tools for your whole team to organize business relationships, manage the sales pipeline, respond to customer support issues, send bulk personalized emails, and gain insights through reporting and analytics - all for free with unlimited contacts. [1] Combining the contactless NFC cards with a capable free CRM could significantly enhance your networking capabilities and contact management workflow.

Founded by Andrea, an experienced learning experience (LX) designer with a background in educational technology, the platform is not just about skill development. Andrea's vision includes making a significant social impact by addressing the digital divide and reducing digital poverty, particularly in rural areas of Wales. Drawing on her self-taught expertise and practical experience, Andrea is addressing the current gap in high-quality, engaging CPD resources tailored to the specific needs of the Welsh school curriculum.

Inspired by successful initiatives like the BYP Network's Black Experience and building on her previous work with Technocamps, Andrea is committed to making this platform CPD-approved and establishing it as the leading provider of digital skills training for non-technical teachers in Wales. [07/03/2025, 11:58:32] Andie: I've reviewed the latest information on the LinkedIn algorithm for 2025, and here are the key takeaways that we need to implement in our strategy:

*Organic reach is down, but engagement is up*: Organic reach has decreased significantly, but engagement per post has increased. This means our content needs to be more engaging to stand out.

*Ad space is increasing*: There are more ads on the platform, so our organic content needs to be even more compelling to compete.

*Frequency and Format Matter*: Posting 1-2 times daily leads to growth. Carousels and PDFs are performing significantly better than other formats.

*Comments are Crucial:* Longer, more thoughtful comments are favored over short or AI-generated ones. Engaging in comments on our own and others' posts is vital.

*Video reach has dropped*: Video reach is down considerably. If we use videos, they must be incredibly engaging.

*Dwell time is key*: Content that keeps users engaged for longer (like infographics and carousels) performs best. Longer captions can also achieve this.

*Top creators post daily:* Top 1% creators post every day, engage heavily, and use well-formatted, dense content (primarily carousels and cheat sheets).

*Action items*:

-Prioritize creating carousels and PDFs.
-Engage with posts regularly, especially our own.Consider the impact of reduced video reach.
-Ensure all posts have strong hooks and data visualization where possible.
-Aim for post lengths of 800-1000 words when appropriate. â€<This message was edited>

 A PRD translates that narrative ("joyful haircare for Black women and girls") into tangible product development efforts. It connects the founder's story to features, UX (user experience) decisions, and manufacturing specs.

Engineers or manufacturers (e.g. specs for the applicator mechanism)

Marketers (e.g. key messages and benefits)

Customer support (e.g. explaining how to use the product)
